The most common threat action variety in global industrial cyber espionage incidents in 2016 was social engineering through phishing, with 181 reported breaches. Hacking using backdoors or command and control (C2) malware was the second most common, with 138 reported breaches. Malware was the most common type of threat, with 471 reported breaches, including 136 for C2 malware and 118 for backdoor malware. Other types of malware included adminware (63 breaches), malware for capturing or exporting data (60 and 53 breaches, respectively), downloaders (53 breaches), and spyware or keyloggers (51 breaches). The least common threat action variety was hacking using stolen credentials, with only 28 reported breaches.

Gen X, which includes individuals born between 1965 and 1981, had 32% of them falling into this category. Finally, Boomers, who are born between 1946 and 1964, had the lowest percentage of impulsive buyers at just 16%.

According to a survey conducted in July 2017, PayPal was considered the most secure money transfer or payment app by users in the United States. Out of the respondents, 74% chose PayPal as the app they perceived to be very secure or somewhat secure. Apple Pay and Google Wallet followed closely, with 40% and 35% of respondents respectively choosing them as the most secure. Samsung Pay and Facebook Messenger Payments were also popular choices, with 29% and 23% of respondents selecting them as the most secure. Venmo and Zelle were also mentioned by some respondents, with 21% and 16% respectively. Finally, PopMoney and Snapcash were the least popular choices, with only 17% of respondents selecting them as the most secure.

This trend suggests that journalists are getting older and may face challenges related to retirement and recruitment of younger replacements.

The statistic shows the average percentage change on the previous year of rent increase in the Netherlands in 2019, by type of rental. The data is presented for both rent harmonization included and excluded.[[SEP]][[SEP]]For total rental, the rent increase including rent harmonization was 2.5%, while the rent increase excluding rent harmonization was 2.1%. The percentages were 51% for Obama and 47% for Romney among this group. The percentages were similar among those with some college education, with 49% for Obama and 48% for Romney. However, Romney received a higher percentage of votes among those with a college degree, 47% for Obama and 51% for Romney. Finally, among those with postgraduate education, 55% voted for Obama and 42% voted for Romney.

The annual average value of retail and wholesale beef in the United States from 2006 to 2019 is shown in this statistic. The retail value is the price that consumers pay for beef at the grocery store, while the wholesale value is the price that grocery stores pay to suppliers for the beef. The retail value is generally higher than the wholesale value because of the costs associated with transportation, storage, and other expenses that are passed on to consumers. The statistic shows that the retail value of beef has been steadily increasing over the past decade, while the wholesale value has been relatively stable.

The Druzhba pipeline, also known as the Friendship Pipeline, is a crude oil pipeline that runs from Russia to several European countries. In 2018, the total volume of crude oil exported through the pipeline was 1,000 barrels per day. The pipeline's capacity is 1 million barrels per day, so the actual volume of oil exported in 2018 was significantly lower than the pipeline's capacity. The countries that received the most oil through the pipeline were Germany, Poland, and the Czech Republic, with each receiving over 200,000 barrels per day. Slovakia and Hungary also received significant amounts of oil, with over 100,000 barrels per day each. The remaining countries received less than 100,000 barrels per day each.

As of April 12, 2020, a majority of Americans believed that doctors should prioritize giving ventilators to patients most in need at the moment and those most likely to recover with treatment, regardless of age. However, there was some variation in opinion by age group. For example, 58% of 18-29 year olds and 50% of 30-49 year olds believed that patients most in need at the moment should be a priority, compared to 57% of 50-64 year olds and 37% of 65+ year olds.

The Battle of Stones River was a significant engagement in the American Civil War, fought in December 1862 and January 1863. The Union Army, led by General William T. Sherman, suffered a total of 129,06 casualties, including 16,77 killed, 7,543 wounded, and 3,686 missing or captured. The Confederate Army, led by General Nathan Bedford Forrest, suffered a total of 11,739 casualties, including 1,294 killed, 7,945 wounded, and 2,500 missing or captured.

In 2018, the global market share for stem cell therapy was divided into two main treatment types: allogenic and autologous. Allogenic therapy, which involves the use of stem cells from a donor, held a larger market share of 64.5%, compared to autologous therapy, which utilizes stem cells from the patient themselves, with a market share of 35.5%. However, by 2029, the market share for autologous therapy is expected to increase to 56%, while allogenic therapy's share will remain at 44%.

According to a recent survey, Facebook and TV are the most common sources of false or inaccurate information regarding the COVID-19 pandemic. The survey found that 78% of respondents said they had seen false information on Facebook, while 37% said they had seen it on TV. In comparison, only 31% of respondents said they had seen false information in newspapers, and 23% said they had seen it in magazines. Radio and Instagram were also common sources of false information, but to a lesser extent. The survey also found that more women than men believed they had seen false information regarding the pandemic.

The percentage of U.S. students' expenses for tuition fees, room, and board covered by Pell grants has been steadily declining over the past two decades. According to data from 2000/2001 to 2020/2021, the coverage rate for public four-year institutions decreased from 39% to 29%, while the coverage rate for private four-year institutions remained relatively stable at around 15%. This trend suggests that the burden of paying for higher education is increasingly falling on students and their families, rather than being shared by the government through Pell grants.

Other popular sites included Dao Dao, Booking.com, Qunar, eLong, and Agoda.
The statistic shows the prevalence of overweight and obese individuals in England in 2019, broken down by region, gender, and gender. The data is presented as a percentage of the respective populations. The regions covered include the North East, North West, Yorkshire and the Humber, East Midlands, West Midlands, East of England, London, South East, and South West. The gender breakdown is provided for both men and women. The statistic highlights the prevalence of overweight and obese individuals across different regions and genders, with some regions and genders having higher rates than others.
In 2014, 29% of customers in Canada were very satisfied with Sears, while in 2016, this number increased to 26%. On the other hand, the percentage of customers who were very dissatisfied with Sears decreased from 9% in 2014 to 10% in 2016.
The number of prisoners in Russia has been steadily increasing over the past few years, with a particularly sharp rise in 2017. The majority of prisoners are Russian nationals, but there is also a significant number of foreigners in the prison population.
A map of the United States shows the predicted outcome of the 2012 presidential election by state. The map is divided into different colored regions, with blue representing states likely to vote for Obama, red representing states likely to vote for Romney, and green representing states that are undecided. The map shows that Obama has a strong lead in states such as California, New York, and Illinois, while Romney has a strong lead in states such as Texas and Florida. The map also shows that several states, including Ohio and Pennsylvania, are considered toss-ups, with both candidates having an equal chance of winning.
The chart shows the average monthly savings as a percentage of average income in Great Britain for different age groups during summer and autumn 2014. The data is presented for six age groups: 65 and over, 55-64, 45-54, 35-44, 25-34, and 16-24.[[SEP]][[SEP]]The chart shows that older individuals tended to save a higher percentage of their income compared to younger individuals. For example, individuals aged 65 and over saved an average of 9.21% of their income during summer 2014 and 8.21% during autumn 2014. In contrast, individuals aged 16-24 saved the lowest percentage of their income, with an average of 8.69% during summer 2014 and 8.56% during autumn
The value of imports and exports of goods in Sint Eustatius, a part of the Caribbean Netherlands, has been steadily increasing since 2012, with a notable jump in 2018. In 2019, the import value reached $45,307, while the export value was $12,693. This indicates a positive trade balance for Sint Eustatius.
A chart showing the percentage of people in Scotland who support independence for their country, with the dates of Nov 2020, Aug 2020, Jan 2020, Apr 2019, Jun 2018, and Jan 2018.
This statistic shows the average hourly pay and tips for massage therapists in the U.S. in 2012, by work setting. The data is presented in U.S. dollars. The work settings include: Hotel / Resort / Cruise, Client's home, Client's workplace, My office, My home, Health club or athletic facility, Spa or salon, Chiropractic office or integrated clinic, Hospital / medical office or clinic, Massage therapy franchise or chain. The average hourly pay ranges from $18.12 to $35.48, and the average tip ranges from 10.51% to 17.48%. The work setting with the highest average hourly pay is Hotel / Resort / Cruise, while the work setting with the highest average tip is Client's home.
The age structure of Bahrain from 2009 to 2019 shows a steady increase in the percentage of the population aged 65 years and older, while the percentage of people aged 15-64 years remains relatively stable. In 2019, 18.72% of the population was aged 0-14 years, 78.76% was aged 15-64 years, and 2.52% was aged 65 years and older. This trend reflects the aging population in Bahrain and the need for policies and programs to support the elderly and maintain a healthy and active population.
In 2018, Disney/Fox and Comcast/Sky spent a significant portion of their content budgets worldwide and in the United States. Disney/Fox allocated 11% of their total content spend to the global market and 23% to the United States market, while Comcast/Sky allocated 9% to the global market and 63% to the United States market. It's worth noting that "Other" companies made up the remaining 80% of the content spend worldwide and 8% in the United States.
The statistic shows the share of U.S. graduates who were indebted due to undergraduate student loans in 2016, by ethnicity. It reveals that a higher percentage of students from certain ethnic groups were indebted compared to others. For example, 68% of white students and 69% of white students were indebted, while 82% of black or African American students and 87% of black or African American students were indebted. Similarly, 61% of Hispanic or Latino students and 72% of Hispanic or Latino students were indebted. The statistic also shows differences in indebtedness based on whether students received a Pell Grant or not, with a higher percentage of students who received a Pell Grant being indebted.
The graph shows the public sector expenditure on health in the United Kingdom from 1996/97 to 2019/20, presented in both nominal and real terms. The data is represented in billions of British Pounds. The trend shows a steady increase in expenditure over the years, with a slight fluctuation in some years. The real-term analysis takes into account inflation, providing a clearer picture of the actual purchasing power of the money spent on healthcare.
The total population of Niger from 2009 to 2019, by gender, is shown in the graph. The graph shows that the population of Niger has been steadily increasing over the years, with a slight increase in the number of females compared to males. In 2019, the population of Niger was 11.6 million, with 5.9 million females and 5.7 million males.
The statistic shows the impact of the single currency euro on the difficulty and cost of travel within the eurozone from 2010 to 2019. It is based on a survey of individuals who have traveled within the eurozone during this period. The respondents were asked to rate the ease of comparing prices between EU countries, the extent to which the euro has made traveling easier and less costly, and the reduction in banking charges when traveling between EU countries. The results are presented as percentages for each year. In general, the majority of respondents found traveling within the eurozone to be easier and less costly due to the single currency. The reduction in banking charges was also noted by a significant number of respondents.
The unemployment rate in Belgium in 2019 varied by region and gender. In the Flemish Region, the rate was 3.3% for males and 3.1% for females. In the Brussels-Capital Region, the rate was 12.8% for males and 12.6% for females. In the Walloon Region, the rate was 8.2% for males and 6% for females.
During the COVID-19 pandemic in the Philippines, food and groceries were the most frequently purchased online, with 66% of female and 66% of male consumers reporting such purchases. Personal hygiene products were also popular, with 52% of female and 47% of male consumers reporting purchases in this category.
According to this survey, 54% of Democrats believe that FOX News has a lot of influence on Donald Trump's decision making, while 27% of Independents and 10% of Republicans agree. However, only 30% of total respondents believe that FOX News has a lot of influence on Trump's decisions.
The number of suicides in Sweden has been steadily increasing over the past decade, with a particularly alarming spike in 2014. In that year, there were 16.3 suicides per 100,000 inhabitants, compared to an average of 13.5 per 100,000 over the previous nine years. The trend is particularly concerning for males, who have consistently had a higher suicide rate than females. However, there has been some improvement in recent years, with the number of suicides decreasing slightly in 2018 and 2019.
The number of betting shops in the UK operated by major companies such as William Hill, Ladbrokes, Gala Coral Group, and Betfred has been steadily declining since 2009. In March 2019, there were 2264 betting shops in the UK, a decrease of 11.4% compared to March 2018. The decline can be attributed to the increasing popularity of online betting and the shift towards more convenient and accessible gambling options.
The statistic shows the distribution of money income of the population in Russia from 2013 to the 2nd quarter of 2020, broken down by source. The sources include paid employee's renumeration, social payments, entrepreneurial activity, property income, and other income. The data is presented as a percentage of the total money income for each year.[[SEP]][[SEP]]In 2013, paid employee's renumeration accounted for the largest portion of money income at 55.1%, followed by social payments at 18.7%, entrepreneurial activity at 7%, property income at 4.7%, and other income at 14.5%.[[SEP]][[SEP]]By 2014, the percentage of money income from paid employee's renumeration had increased to 54.9%, while social payments had decreased to 18.2%. This statistic shows the employment in the U.S. motion picture and video industry from 2009 to 2017, broken down by sector. The sector includes motion picture and video distribution, postproduction services and other motion picture and video industries, motion picture and video exhibition, and motion picture and video production. The data is presented in thousands, with each sector's employment levels for each year shown in the table. Overall, the industry saw a slight decline in employment from 2009 to 2017, with the exception of a slight increase in 2016.
The top 10 leading ports in the United States in 2018, ranked by tonnage, are shown in the table. The top port, Port of South Louisiana, handled over 141 million tons of cargo, followed by Houston with over 191 million tons. New York and New Jersey were third with over 93 million tons, and Beaumont was fourth with over 61 million tons. Other ports on the list include Corpus Christi, Long Beach, Baton Rouge, and the Port of Virginia.
The statistic shows the dependency of leading defense suppliers on the Ministry of Defense (MOD) business in the United Kingdom (UK) from 2005/06 to 2019/20. The data is presented in a bar chart with the year on the x-axis and the companies listed on the y-axis. The companies included in the chart are QinetiQ Group PLC, Babcock International Group PLC, BAE Systems PLC, Ferrovial SA, Leonardo SpA, Rolls-Royce Holdings PLC, General Dynamics Corporation, Lockheed Martin Corporation, Airbus Group SE, and The Boeing Company. The chart shows that the dependency of these companies on MOD business has been decreasing over the years, with the exception of a slight increase in 2019/20.
The statistic shows the percentage of new drug applications (NDAs/BLAs) that were ultimately approved in select disease areas in the United States between 2006 and 2015. The data is presented in a bar chart with the disease areas listed on the x-axis and the approval rates on the y-axis. The chart shows that the approval rates varied across disease areas, with oncology, allergy, respiratory, and cardiovascular having the highest approval rates on first and second review. In contrast, the approval rates for infectious disease, urology, autoimmune, metabolic, ophthalmology, and hematology were lower but still relatively high. The chart also shows that the overall approval rate for all diseases was 61% on first review, 80% on second review, and 86% overall.
A breakdown of MLB fans in the United States by ethnicity as of August 2020. White fans make up the largest group at 47%, followed by Hispanic fans at 29%, African American fans at 24%, and other ethnicities at 54%.
The statistic shows the rate of organ transplantation activity per million population in Estonia from 2017 to 2019, by organ type. The data is presented in a bar chart with five bars, one for each organ type. The bars are labeled with the organ type and the corresponding values for 2017, 2018, and 2019.[[SEP]][[SEP]]The chart shows that the most common organ type for transplantation in Estonia is the kidney, with a rate of 26.9, 44.6, and 31.5 per million population in 2017, 2018, and 2019, respectively. The liver is the second most common organ type, with a rate of 7.7, 7.7, and 7.7 per million population in the same years. The lung is the least common
In many countries, including Hong Kong, South Korea, Japan, and New Zealand, the actual percentage of deaths among women aged 15 to 24 that were suicide was higher than the average guess of respondents. For example, in Hong Kong, the actual rate was 14%, but the average guess was 50%. This highlights the importance of raising awareness and providing support for those at risk of suicide.
The revenue of Miele & Cie. in Germany has been steadily increasing over the past few years, with a slight dip in 2017/18. Despite this, the company remains a major player in the international market, with a significant portion of its revenue coming from outside of Germany.
The market share of smartphones in the United States from 2017 to 2019, by display size. The data shows a decline in the market share for smartphones with a display size of less than 4.5 inches, while the market share for smartphones with a display size of 6 inches or more continues to grow.
According to this statistic, 84% of parents set rules for their children when using smartphones or tablets. These rules include not arranging to meet someone they've only met online, not talking to strangers, not sharing personal information, and telling their parents if something worries them. Additionally, 80% of parents also set rules about spending money and being respectful to others online. Other rules that may be set include limiting screen time, only allowing certain apps, and requiring permission before downloading an app.
The graph shows the revenue generated by Pandora from 2006 to 2019, broken down by source. The sources include advertising, subscription services and other, and ticketing service. The revenue for each year is shown in millions of U.S. dollars. The graph shows that the revenue from advertising has been steadily increasing over the years, while the revenue from subscription services and other has been increasing and decreasing at different times. The ticketing service has been unprofitable for Pandora since 2014.
The statistic shows the number of fatalities in traffic accidents in Belgium in 2019, broken down by age group and region. The data is presented in a bar chart with the age groups ranging from 0 to 75 and the regions consisting of the Flemish Region, Brussels-Capital Region, and Walloon Region. The chart reveals that the majority of fatalities occurred among individuals aged 20 to 44, with the Brussels-Capital Region experiencing the highest number of fatalities overall. The Flemish Region had the lowest number of fatalities, with only one occurrence.
The average movie ticket price at AMC Theatres worldwide increased from $9.61 in 2015 to $9.67 in 2017, but decreased to $8.04 in 2016. In 2019, the price increased to $9.54 in the United States and $8.61 in international regions.
The graph shows the number of OTC readers and contact lenses purchased worldwide in 2013, by country. The United States leads the way with the highest number of readers and contact lenses purchased, followed by Germany and Italy. Spain and the United Kingdom also show significant purchases in this category. France has a lower but still notable number of purchases.
The total number of microloans distributed in the United Kingdom from 2012 to 2017, by purpose.
The share of Saint Lucia's economic sectors in its gross domestic product (GDP) has remained relatively stable over the past decade. In 2019, the agricultural sector contributed 2.01% to the GDP, while the industry and services sectors contributed 9.97% and 75.18%, respectively. These figures are similar to those from previous years, with only minor fluctuations in the contributions of each sector. Overall, the services sector has consistently been the largest contributor to Saint Lucia's GDP, while the agricultural sector has remained relatively stable.
In March and April 2020, 60% of Russians surveyed said they would be willing to sacrifice some of their rights in order to contain the spread of COVID-19. This number increased to 69% in April.
The age structure of the Philippines from 2009 to 2019 shows a steady increase in the proportion of the population aged 65 years and older, while the proportion of those aged 0-14 years and 15-64 years remains relatively stable. In 2019, 30.48% of the population was aged 0-14 years, 64.21% was aged 15-64 years, and 5.31% was aged 65 years and older. This trend reflects the country's aging population and potential challenges related to healthcare and social security.
The value of ginger imports and exports in the Netherlands from 2008 to 2019. The exports consistently exceeded the imports during this period, with the exception of 2012. The highest export value was in 2019, at 94,735 euros, while the highest import value was in 2018, at 87,463 euros.
The consumption of yogurt with and without additives per person increased steadily from 2010 to 2019. In 2019, the volume of yogurt with additives consumed per person was 2.78 kilograms, while the volume of yogurt without additives consumed per person was 7.02 kilograms.
The annual amount of heat pumps in operation in Ireland increased steadily from 2013 to 2019. In 2019, there were a total of 41,158 heat pumps in operation, with 36,436 being aerothermal heat pumps and 4,722 being ground source heat pumps.
In the period between 2013 and 2014 in Paris, 100% of rape cases involving adult victims were reported, while 4% of rape cases involving minor victims were reported.
The statistic shows the share of electoral college votes for the Democratic and Republican parties in presidential elections from 1860 to 2020. The data is presented in a bar chart with the years on the x-axis and the shares of votes for each party on the y-axis. The chart shows that the Democratic party generally received more votes than the Republican party, with a few exceptions. In 2020, for example, the Democratic party received 56.88% of the electoral college votes, while the Republican party received 43.12%. The chart also shows that the percentage of votes for each party has varied over time, with some years favoring one party over the other.
The statistic shows the percentage of people who have a favorable opinion of Israel and the Palestinian Authority from 2000 to 2012. In 2012, 71% of people had a favorable opinion of Israel, while 19% had an unfavorable opinion. For the Palestinian Authority, 68% of people had a favorable opinion, and 19% had an unfavorable opinion. The trend shows a slight increase in favorable opinions of both Israel and the Palestinian Authority over the years, with a few exceptions.
The statistic shows the percentage of people who consider different arrangements to be a family or not. It is based on four different scenarios: married couple with children (99% consider it a family), married couple without children (88% consider it a family), single parent with children (86% consider it a family), and unmarried couple with children (80% consider it a family). Additionally, the statistic includes same-sex couples with and without children, with 63% and 45% respectively considering it a family. The remaining 34% and 52% of same-sex couples do not consider it a family. Lastly, the statistic also shows the percentage of unmarried couples without children (43%) and same-sex couples without children (45%) who do not consider it a family.
According to this statistic, 60% of males and 69% of females watch football on TV for 5 hours or less per week during the NFL season. Meanwhile, 27% of males and 31% of females watch for 6-10 hours per week, and 7% of both genders watch for 11-15 hours per week. Finally, 6% of both genders watch for 16 hours or more per week.
The chart shows the percentage of people in selected European countries who trust news organizations and journalists. In Finland, 62% of people trust news organizations, while in Germany, only 47% of people trust journalists. The numbers are similar in Denmark, where 47% of people trust news organizations and 40% trust journalists. In the United Kingdom, 42% of people trust news organizations and 29% trust journalists. In Ireland, 47% of people trust news organizations and 37% trust journalists. In France, 28% of people trust news organizations and 29% trust journalists. In Italy, 43% of people trust news organizations and 33% trust journalists. In Spain, 43% of people trust news organizations and 35% trust journalists.
The average speed on roads in Great Britain in 2014 varied depending on the vehicle type and road type. On built-up roads, the average speed was 30 mph for cars and motorcycles, while it was slightly higher at 36 mph on 40 mph built-up roads. On motorways, the average speed was 68 mph for all vehicles, while on dual carriageways, it was slightly lower at 67 mph. On single carriageways, the average speed was 51 mph for cars and 47 mph for motorcycles.
The most underserved airline routes in the US in 2015, by type of booking, show that non-stop bookings were more common than one-stop bookings. The top five most underserved routes were from Boston to Orlando, Las Vegas, San Francisco, Los Angeles, and Tampa. The least served routes were from Los Angeles to Philadelphia and Las Vegas to Orlando.
The number of airplanes in aviation companies in Germany increased steadily from 2007 to 2019, with the highest number of airplanes recorded in 2019 at 223. The take-off weight of the airplanes also increased over the years, with the largest number of airplanes weighing between 14 and 20 tons in 2019.
The statistic shows the number of news articles and broadcasts regarding the COVID-19 pandemic in Italy between February and March 2020, broken down by channel. The x-axis represents the dates, and the y-axis represents the number of news articles or broadcasts for each channel. The channels included in the statistic are newspapers and magazines, internet, and radio and TV. The data shows a significant increase in news coverage as the pandemic progressed, with the highest number of news articles and broadcasts occurring in the last week of March.
The distribution of digital video advertising impressions in the Asia Pacific region from 1st quarter 2014 to 3rd quarter 2014, by industry, shows that the CPG/FMCG industry accounted for 50% of the impressions in Q1 2014, 35% in Q2 2014, and 34% in Q3 2014. The retail industry accounted for 23% of the impressions in Q1 2014, 17% in Q2 2014, and 22% in Q3 2014. The non-alcoholic beverages industry had 0% of the impressions in Q1 2014, 21% in Q2 2014, and 11% in Q3 2014.
The Sacramento Kings have seen a steady increase in their Facebook and Twitter fan bases since 2012. In September 2020, the team had 7.8 million Facebook fans and 1.0 million Twitter followers, while in March 2020, they had 7.96 million Facebook fans and 1.08 million Twitter followers. The team's popularity has remained relatively consistent over the years, with occasional fluctuations in both fan bases.
The number of attendances in the accident and emergency (A&E) departments in Northern Ireland in March 2020, by waiting time.
This statistic shows the share of people participating and willing to participate in crowdfunding worldwide in 2014, by generation. The results show that millennials are the most likely to participate in crowdfunding, with 47% saying they have given or are likely to give. Gen X is not far behind, with 30% saying they have given or are likely to give. Boomers are less likely to participate, with only 13% saying they have given or are likely to give. The smallest group, matures, shows only 2% saying they have given or are likely to give.
The value of macadamia nut imports and exports in the Netherlands from 2008 to 2019. The exports consistently outpaced the imports during this period, with the exception of 2015 when the import value was higher than the export value. The overall trend shows an increase in both import and export values over the years, with a slight dip in 2015.
In this survey, 92% of very liberal respondents preferred Hillary Clinton over Donald Trump, while 7% preferred Trump. Among somewhat liberal respondents, 87% chose Clinton and 8% chose Trump, with 5% not sure. Among moderates, 50% preferred Clinton and 37% preferred Trump, with 14% not sure. Among somewhat conservative respondents, 9% chose Clinton and 88% chose Trump, with 3% not sure. Among very conservative respondents, only 4% chose Clinton and 95% chose Trump, with 0% not sure.
In 2018, 29% of U.S. adults reported that they were likely to use genetic testing to determine their cancer risk in the future, with the majority of this group using genetic testing ordered by a doctor or genetic specialist. Additionally, 35% of adults reported that they were somewhat likely to use genetic testing, and 28% were very likely to use it. Only 12% of adults reported that they were not likely at all to use genetic testing for cancer risk determination.
The statistic shows the share of retail revenue from foreign operations of the world's 250 leading retailers from 2009 to 2018, by product sector. The data is presented as a percentage of total revenue.[[SEP]][[SEP]]In 2018, the largest share of retail revenue came from the Apparel & accessories sector, with 38.5% of the total revenue. The Hardlines and leisure goods sector followed with 22.2%, while the FMCG sector accounted for 11.4% of the total revenue.[[SEP]][[SEP]]The trend of increasing foreign revenue share over the years is evident from the data. In 2009, the share of foreign revenue was 24.7%, which increased to 25.1% in 2010, and continued to grow until it reached 38.

The value of durian imports and exports in the Netherlands has fluctuated over the past 12 years, with a notable increase in 2019. In that year, the import value reached 1761 thousand euros, while the export value was 1240 thousand euros. This indicates that more durians were imported into the Netherlands than were exported, potentially suggesting a growing demand for this fruit in the Dutch market.
The statistic shows the average stumpage prices for various species of trees in the United States from 2002 to 2015. The prices are shown in U.S. dollars per 1,000 board feet. The species included in the statistic are: Douglas-fir, Southern pine, Ponderosa pine, Western hemlock, and all eastern hardwoods. Additionally, the prices for oak, white, red, and black are also shown separately. The prices for each year are shown in the table, with the prices for 2015 being the highest at $69.04 per 1,000 board feet for Douglas-fir.
The statistic shows the number of active physicians in the U.S. in 2017, grouped by medical specialty and gender. There were a total of 78,659 active physicians in the U.S. in 2017, with the majority of them practicing in internal medicine (43,770) and family medicine/general practice (68,004). Among male physicians, there were more in the specialties of anesthesiology (10,624) and emergency medicine (11,658), while among female physicians, there were more in the specialties of obstetrics & gynecology (23,740) and family medicine/general practice (45,342). The statistic provides a detailed breakdown of the medical specialties and the distribution of active physicians by gender.
In 2013, the portfolio of sustainable and responsible investments (SRI) in Finland consisted mainly of bonds, which made up 49% of the total assets. In 2015, the SRI portfolio consisted of a higher percentage of equity, with 38% of the assets being in this asset type. Real estate made up 7% of the assets in both years, while other assets made up 6% in 2013 and 2.15% in 2015. Alternative investments made up 5.75% of the assets in 2013 and 2.62% in 2015. Venture capital/private equity made up 0% of the assets in both years.
The frequency of betting as a gambling activity in the United Kingdom has remained relatively stable over the past four years. In 2016, 25% of respondents reported betting on sports or other events at least twice a week, while in 2019, this figure remained at 24.3%. The majority of respondents (30.9% in 2016, 26.7% in 2017, 31.9% in 2018, and 28.1% in 2019) reported betting once a week or less often. Interestingly, the percentage of respondents who reported betting less than once a month increased slightly over the four-year period, from 20% in 2016 to 25.7% in 2019.
In 2017, 47.1% of high school students overall were trying to lose weight. This figure was higher for females (59.9%) than for males (34%), and varied by ethnicity. White (non-Hispanic) students were the most likely to be trying to lose weight (58.6%), followed by Black (non-Hispanic) students (55.3%), and Hispanic students (65.6%).
The statistic shows the number of employees in various sectors in Poland in 2020, with a focus on the sectors most affected by the restrictions due to the COVID-19 pandemic. The sectors include trade and repair of motor vehicles, transport and storage, administration and support activities, accommodation and catering, and other service activities. The data is presented in thousands, with the total number of employees in all sectors reaching 1,000,000. The sectors with the highest number of employees are trade and repair of motor vehicles, followed by transport and storage, and accommodation and catering. The sectors with the lowest number of employees are "Culture, entertainment, recreation" and other service activities.
In the Philippines, 37% of female respondents and 28% of male respondents reported engaging in panic buying due to the COVID-19 pandemic as of April 2020.
The poverty headcount rate in Nigeria in 2019 varied by area and household size. In urban areas, the poverty rate was highest for households with 20 or more people, at 71.57%, while in rural areas, the rate was highest for households with 10-19 people, at 44.47%. The poverty rate was lowest for households of 1 person in both urban and rural areas, at 1.66% and 5.23% respectively.
The statistic shows the enrollment numbers of kindergarten and nursery school in the United States from 1980 to 2018, broken down by type of attendance. The data is presented in thousands, with the year on the x-axis and the full-day and half-day attendance on the y-axis. The trend shows a steady increase in enrollment numbers over the years, with a slight fluctuation in some years. In 2018, the enrollment numbers reached 5,015,000 for full-day attendance and 2,733,000 for half-day attendance.
The global crop protection market experienced a significant increase from 2006 to 2012, with a nominal growth rate of 7.4% in 2012 and a real growth rate of 10%. This outpaces the growth of the overall agricultural market, which saw a nominal growth rate of 2.8% in 2012. The market experienced a slight decline in 2009, with a nominal growth rate of 0.2%, but rebounded strongly in 2010 with a nominal growth rate of 1.2%. The market continued to grow steadily until 2012, when it experienced a slight decline, with a nominal growth rate of 7.4% and a real growth rate of 10%.
The graph shows the number of Facebook fans and Twitter followers for the Orlando Magic NBA team from September 2012 to September 2020. The team's Facebook fans increased steadily over the years, while Twitter followers remained relatively stable. The highest number of Facebook fans was reached in September 2020 with 2.7 million, and the highest number of Twitter followers was reached in March 2020 with 1.51 million.
The chart shows the number of Facebook fans and Twitter followers for the Houston Texans NFL team from August 2012 to August 2020. The team's Facebook fans increased steadily over the years, while their Twitter followers remained relatively stable. The highest number of Facebook fans was reached in August 2020 with 2.16 million, and the highest number of Twitter followers was reached in February 2020 with 1.9 million.
In 2017, there were a total of 89 deaths caused by alcoholic liver disease in Northern Ireland. The majority of these deaths occurred among individuals aged 45-49 (16 deaths), followed by those aged 50-54 (11 deaths). There were also a significant number of deaths among individuals aged 35-39 (7 deaths) and 40-44 (11 deaths). Interestingly, there were no deaths reported among individuals aged 20-24. The data also shows that there were more deaths among men than women, with a total of 19 more deaths among men.
The number of employees at Acer increased steadily from 2016 to 2020, with the largest growth occurring in the Sales & Product Marketing and Research & Development departments. The company also saw an increase in administration and customer service employees.
According to a recent survey, respondents were asked how they expected COVID-19 to impact their spending for various technologies. For cybersecurity, 84% of respondents expected an increase, while only 3% expected a decrease. Similarly, for hybrid or multi-cloud, 74% expected an increase, and only 7% expected a decrease. A new statistic has been released showing the most popular boating activities for both males and females. According to the data, fishing from a boat is the most popular activity for both genders, with 46.6% of females and 66.1% of males reporting that they have done this activity. Cruising is also a popular activity, with 49.7% of females and 57.3% of males enjoying this pastime. Swimming is another popular activity, with 46% of females and 44.9% of males participating. Entertaining is also a common activity, with 46.6% of females and 39.8% of males engaging in this activity. Other popular activities include sightseeing, nature observation, and quiet water paddling.
According to a survey conducted in June 2016 in the United States, the most important online safety topics for parents of online teens and online teens themselves were preventing identity theft and keeping devices secure. Other important topics included learning how to identify fake emails, social posts, and texts, as well as understanding the risks of sexting. Parents and teens also expressed interest in learning how to report serious problems they encounter online and how to manage their privacy online. Additionally, there was a desire to learn how to block people and deal with bullies, as well as how to adjust settings on social networks and begin conversations with parents or children about staying safe online.

The number of full car driving license holders among all adults in England has increased steadily over the past few decades. In 1975/76, there were only 6.0 million full car driving license holders, while in 2019, there were 16.0 million for females and 17.0 million for males, indicating a significant growth in the number of people with driving licenses. The trend shows that more and more people are obtaining their driving licenses, which could be attributed to various factors such as increased access to driving education, changes in transportation needs, and government policies that encourage driving as a means of transportation.
The gender parity index for gross enrollment ratios in primary, secondary, and tertiary education in developing regions in 2012 shows that Sub-Saharan Africa has the lowest ratio in primary education (0.92) and secondary education (0.84), while Oceania has the lowest ratio in all three levels of education (0.93). Western Asia has the highest ratio in primary education (0.93), while Northern Africa has the highest ratio in all three levels of education (0.96). Latin America & the Caribbean has the highest ratio in primary education (0.99), while Southern Asia has the highest ratio in secondary education (0.93). The developing regions have the highest ratio in tertiary education (1.0), but the lowest ratio in primary education (0.97).

A new survey has found that the way people conduct themselves in advertising can greatly influence consumer purchasing intent. The study, conducted in March 2020, found that people were much more likely to be influenced by ads that showed people hugging, kissing, and shaking hands than those that showed them standing more than 6 feet apart or participating in video calls or practicing "social distancing." The most influential ads were those that showed people hugging and kissing, with 58% of respondents saying they were more likely to make a purchase as a result.

The installed capacity of sites generating electricity from renewable sources in the United Kingdom increased from 2018 to 2019. The largest increase came from wind energy, which saw a capacity increase of 23.1 megawatts electrical. Solar PV saw a slight increase as well, with a capacity increase of 1.2 megawatts electrical. Other bioenergy, hydro, landfill gas, and sewage gas all saw slight decreases in capacity. The total installed capacity of renewable energy sites in the UK increased from 44,340.4 megawatts electrical in 2018 to 47,162.8 megawatts electrical in 2019.

In 2018, Tamil Nadu in India reported a prevalence of various types of disabilities among its population. The most common type of disability was locomotor disability, affecting 1.2% of the male population and 1% of the female population. Hearing and visual disabilities were also prevalent, affecting 0.3% and 0.2% of the population, respectively. Mental retardation/intellectual disability and mental illness were less common, affecting 0.2% and 0.1% of the population, respectively. The remaining types of disabilities, such as speech and language disability and other types of disability, affected a smaller proportion of the population.

However, men were more likely to engage in activities such as making video or voice calls over the internet, playing or downloading games, and watching video content from services such as YouTube, while women were more likely to use social networking and look for health-related information. The distribution of life insurance premiums supply channels in Bulgaria from 2012 to 2018 shows a shift towards direct writing. In 2012, 18.7% of premiums were generated through direct writing, while brokers and agents accounted for 39.3% and 42.9% respectively. By 2018, the percentages had changed, with direct writing accounting for 42.54%, brokers for 41.16%, and agents for 77%. This indicates a trend towards more direct sales of life insurance policies in Bulgaria.

A comparison of average daily in-home data usage in the United States by device type in March 2019 and March 2020. The grand total increased from 12.0 gigabytes in 2019 to 16.6 gigabytes in 2020. Streaming Boxes/Sticks saw the largest increase, going from 3.9 gigabytes to 5.4 gigabytes. Gaming consoles also saw a significant increase, going from 3.0 gigabytes to 4.4 gigabytes. Connected TVs experienced a slight increase, going from 2.6 gigabytes to 3.6 gigabytes. PC/Mac usage remained relatively stable, increasing only slightly from 1.4 gigabytes to 1.6 gigabytes. Phone usage increased dramatically, going from 0.7 gigabytes to 1.
